cd autotest/
gradle clean assembleDebug
adb install -r  ./build/apk/autotest-debug-unaligned.apk
adb install -r <THE APK YOU WANT TO TEST>
adb shell "am instrument -w co.tmgamer.automation/<YOU NEED TO TYPE THE PACKAGE NAME IN TO HERE>.TMGTester"

how to use adb devices from remote (test) machines
ssh tmg@192.168.1.246 -C -L 5037:localhost:5037

To block the apps:
adb shell am broadcast -a co.tmgamer.drmapi.BACKDOOR -d drm://OVERRIDE_BLOCK/true
To unblock the apps:
adb shell am broadcast -a co.tmgamer.drmapi.BACKDOOR -d drm://OVERRIDE_BLOCK/false
